# 【2026】尼日利亚 - Teutonique

来源：https://www.yuque.com/chaofun/tuxun/nigeria_teutonique

# 第零章   前言

总结：尼日利亚是一个背路国家

在观看本文档时使用手机排版可能会有些问题，请谅解

本教程旨在教会大家有关尼日利亚的详细区猜技巧，如仅想学习其国家辨识与大致区猜方法，请到Plonk It里先行学习

想要了解大体的区猜方法，可以选择每一节中的总体环境部分先行学习

     尼日利亚是一个幅员辽阔的世界大国（可能并不是），作为一名图寻/Geoguessr玩家，分毫必争，学习它的紧迫性不亚于美加（不可能），但是在国外及国内的各大平台上（不过我没有进专业的社区），有关其的相关教程较少，目前较为完整的是Plonk It上的尼日利亚文档(请原谅我弱到爆的寻找资料的能力)，但它能帮助到我们尼日利亚区猜的题目占比可能还不到10%。而且，经过观察，绝大多数的寻友（小到刚入坑的萌新，大到全球榜前几），在遇到尼日利亚题时都是点中间，不进行区猜，而在匹配中，通过尼日利亚区猜，运气好无倍率可以打掉对面1000+血。所以说学好尼日利亚，绝地反杀便又能多一重可能。经作者的研究，尼日利亚的技巧已较为完整(并非)，故在此向诸位呈上。

 本教程因部分道路跨州，有些区域景观相似，故不按照行政区划，而是按照笔者的愚见笼统地讲解，请您谅解

     因设备问题，早期做的范围图有许多需要改进的地方，我将会在之后努力改进，但不影响学习

     因制作该文档时时间较赶，仍有许多Meta还未写完(有作者的待完成标记)或还没开始写，这将在后续不断更新

    但不得不承认，本文档仍有许多未完善的部分，作者在编写过程中也难免有些许遗漏和错误(尤其是植被部分)，还望大家指正，在此也向大家致歉。

    欢迎大家对本文章提出建议和补充

    祝愿您们能学得愉快！

# 第一章   国家概况

关于尼日利亚，技巧的优先级大致为景观>文字信息>基础设施>街景车=跟车，在本教程中，所以街景车和跟车技巧都是基于环境而论的，它们是在大致区域猜测之后进行更进一步的详细区猜迫不得已才能用到的。在实战中，奇怪的环境和街景车、跟车特例是不可避免的，但还是请你相信景观所透露的信息

难度：ShitcamV2>老Sc>G3>G4

尼日利亚作为一个西非国家，以热带草原气候为主，很多地方分干湿两季，旱季和雨季景观差异极大，且相机代数众多，景观多样，区猜难度非常之大

（关于尼日利亚的国家辨识技巧，因为Plonk It文档已讲得较为充分，这里就不多赘述，如果您觉得本章的信息无法帮助您有效地辨别该国，请先移步至Plonk It)

![呢嫩.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/53025226/1742090358682-f7d742be-1355-48bb-9e42-063e3b797b38.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_29%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

下图为中译的行政区划图（来源百度）
注：本教程以上方的区划图为基准，下图区划部分标准较旧(有误)仅作为部分州名的中译参考

![微信图片_20250726170341.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/53025226/1753520663053-424d85dd-e3c2-49c7-a4ca-6581006b9d0b.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_35%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

尼日利亚，位于西非东南部，非洲几内亚湾西岸的顶点，西与贝宁接壤，北与尼日尔相邻，东与乍得和喀麦隆毗连，南濒大西洋几内亚湾，国土面积923768平方公里，2024年人口为2．27亿，有250多个民族，首都位于阿布贾，全国共有1个联邦首都区、36个州​

![Nigerian-deforrestation-b.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/53025226/1753427614485-ad166782-e65a-4a96-aabd-f721d91b1c49.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_28%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

如图，为尼日利亚的植被演变情况，大体为南多北少

![局部截取_20250726_213026.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753536659198-6d5b013d-45d4-4193-993f-975a1f84ae52.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_18%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

尼日利亚的街景覆盖情况

![局部截取_20250316_102628.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1742092144463-8331478f-c0af-42ba-835e-0928a50a3568.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_30%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![局部截取_20250316_102734.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1742092192986-ce7a2f9c-8431-4823-8f56-c1a36f5bc4bc.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_31%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![局部截取_20250316_102839.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1742092230924-4abbf826-b92b-4236-8242-9eba46cc6334.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_31%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

街景车和代数绝对是辨别尼日利亚非常好的方法

尼日利亚有四种不同的代数覆盖，分别为shitcamV2,shitcam,3代和4代，且相较其他街景车来讲均为特殊街景车   （详见后文）

（关于它们的覆盖范围，详见Plonk It文档或后文）

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1742093824523-f8e205c6-70d6-4bd2-b72f-78c4cad3d15d.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_55%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

车牌如图所示，打码后通体泛绿

![局部截取_20250323_101023.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1742695847108-1dfa47b1-e6f4-48b0-8a68-1dbfe09e8044.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_29%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

在尼日利亚，80%以上的题目都可以见到一辆警车跟车，

警车形式多样（比如涂装黑或白，车型轿车或皮卡等），感兴趣的可以自己研究（因为都很常见，研究了并没有太大的用途)

![局部截取_20250323_103845.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1742697537222-9800353d-acf4-4d48-ad88-adee5f8529a5.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_12%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

尼日利亚原为英殖民地，英语为其官方语言，故在其境内英语是最常见的语言

![局部截取_20250323_192422.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1742729094907-3da3d39e-eb41-4ba3-b463-daa74a72c95d.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_16%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

其电线杆类似与巴西，只不过其上方并没有小孔(并不是一定所有电线杆都长这样）

由于尼日利亚的建筑和环境较为复杂，本章就不再概述，详见后文

因为尼日利亚各代数街景车分布有限，本文故以街景车代数分章，便于学习（不适应的可按个人喜好阅读）

有备注改的都是很久之前写的，请勿参考

## Part1 路灯

只选取常见的、较有代表性的

粗体加下划线表示较为重要

初学者可先跳过

### 贡贝州(Gombe)

Gombe(贡贝)

# 第三章   Gen4(四代）

如果只想简单学习，可以从每一小节的

出租车与嘟嘟车部分和总体环境部分先开始学习

## Part1 绪论

### 四代相机分布概况

尼日利亚的四代街景是尼日利亚分布最广(截至2022年）也是最好进行区域猜测的街景种类，它的分布大体如下图所示

![](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2024/png/35193536/1712942274133-111d451a-7eb8-4da0-a082-fab33d94067e.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_68%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_68%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

不难发现，它的街景主要集中在西南，东南和北方

所以我们可以以尼日尔河为界，进行分区域讨论

![局部截取_20250725_154036.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753429373856-d7cca729-e5b5-4686-aa2d-36a1de253a67.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_18%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

（尼日尔河的位置可以此图为参照，蓝色的就是）

### 不同街景车的分布范围

尼日利亚四代的街景车种类多样，主要有以下四类(覆盖范围不建议学习）

除全码车外，其他车均为尼日利亚特有

#### 1.普通白车

![局部截取_20250725_152225.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753440754296-b6c9974b-d0fe-4164-8841-4e81bc6d6c2d.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_16%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

覆盖范围最广，基本所有地方均可见，有时在其左侧会有一条黄黑相间的条带

#### 2.全码车

![局部截取_20250725_152423.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753440968436-0beb1a1c-ccf5-4ed0-ad77-0dad90c14ba7.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_20%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

通常不会有卡车的拖斗露出，如下图

![局部截取_20250725_152353.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753441070328-5b5a5001-722c-4b34-bd95-ee9c87407fd1.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_29%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

覆盖和普通白车一样，基本所有地方均可见

#### 3.红车(改)(请勿参考)

![局部截取_20250725_152532.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753441369754-2fa5d9b8-4fe2-4622-999c-09e196466d03.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_16%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

#### 4.特殊白车(多条带)(改)(请勿参考)

![局部截取_20250725_153250.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753442910089-af91de87-570c-4b40-a1b3-3d7091a1133b.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_17%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

#### 5.绿水桶车(待完成)

#### 与其他国家的辨别

1.警车跟车；2.皮卡车；3.街景车最右边通常有一根向右前方的天线

## Part2 北部

### 联邦首都区(核心)(FCT)

邀请你来图寻做「联邦首都区G4」题库 [https://tuxun.fun/map/40262](https://tuxun.fun/map/40262)

联邦首都区街景覆盖情况

![屏幕截图 2025-08-16 223206.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1755354753677-7bc5d30b-ce41-47bb-9044-7b370350af78.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_30%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

#### 出租车与嘟嘟车

联邦首都区出租车涂装有两种，其中一种如下图

![局部截取_20250726_181038.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753524757666-f1cd3c22-9ddd-47af-b4e3-2cb10120e323.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_12%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![局部截取_20250726_181127.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753524768880-03c4b511-d6c6-435c-962e-b06bb26fc771.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_12%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

其中绿色色块基本固定为上下两种，其他颜色可变化，通常为为白，橙，蓝等

![局部截取_20250730_143926.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753857714706-af6f52d0-8c0f-4d04-a6a0-718381c5c65f.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_13%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

另一种涂装，车身通体为绿色，从左右车灯各会引出两条白线至尾灯，见下图

注：出租车的车型并不一致，但他们的涂装较为固定

![局部截取_20250730_144038.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753858013862-73b6a3b1-1e69-459e-8500-9be4e3f47bc5.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_20%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

彩蛋！特殊涂装！(也许全阿布贾就它一辆)

![屏幕截图 2025-08-18 132517.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1755499516389-a41cc763-d5a0-4281-a088-70f55fcf3903.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_38%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

在阿布贾的城市郊区及其卫星城市有时可以见到嘟嘟车(涂装多为普通涂装)

![局部截取_20250730_140146.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753855349040-52df7120-e4b6-4990-903f-1367527c3d25.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_11%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

在联邦首都区里，阿布贾作为尼日利亚的首都兼全国第三大城市，时常也可以看见一些嘟嘟车变体，如下图(类似高原州涂装)

![局部截取_20250730_140623.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753855653839-495377b5-a599-4ce4-8dfe-86b00dd186d8.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_13%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![局部截取_20250730_135340.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753855366268-1ba4aa16-6d74-4f3f-844b-3447afe46f44.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_12%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

高原州嘟嘟车可参照下图

它与高原州嘟嘟车的可参见其正面，涂装的范围略有不同；当然也可以看背面，联邦的背面要么全黄要么全绿，而高原州涂色固定，上黄下绿

请注意二者的区分

![局部截取_20250730_141704.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753856404299-927de864-d7e9-4c03-be07-bfbc89185a8d.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_11%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![局部截取_20250730_141709.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753856416065-f4da0a20-da6d-4860-968b-56b839989113.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_11%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

还会出现两地涂装拼搭的情况，如下图(卡杜纳州的浅绿色涂装+高原州与联邦首都区四不像的亮绿色涂装)

![局部截取_20250730_140645.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753855795504-9fa84917-59ac-4fb8-adaa-260d5b329cc3.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_11%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

既然是首都，见到外地嘟嘟车也很正常啦(尤其是邻州)

![屏幕截图 2025-08-18 144147.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1755499352059-c3816e7b-e4c6-454f-b4eb-38f6bf82ba52.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_24%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

有时可以在车身上看到联邦首都区的英文简写(FCT)

#### 总体环境

乡间的路旁常见蒯草(Scirpus cyperinus)，其茎上部截面呈三角形，叶鞘封闭，秋季茎叶转为深褐色，或称香附子、羊毛草等【联邦首都区街景多为秋季拍摄(11月)】

![局部截取_20250726_203044.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753534707460-4f6c0d84-8419-463e-9bfb-0c4160933942.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_20%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

下图为蒯草(来源网络)

![3801213fb80e7bec54e7d85f577aae389b504fc23d4a-bkimg-process,v_1,rw_1,rh_1,maxl_400,pad_1.webp](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/webp/53025226/1753546129543-40b85acc-97ad-4295-b704-364e629a5465.webp?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_11%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

周边经常会见到许多大山和小丘

![局部截取_20250726_203125.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753535048423-8d242c6b-2496-4f92-8bd8-c0a8906885b2.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

农业用地居多，大多数种植玉米，且玉米种植相对稀疏

![局部截取_20250725_222622.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753453752306-6c64c8e7-6d53-4e22-be5e-303ef3261149.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_29%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

土壤通常为黄褐色且会有一点点红和白

![局部截取_20250725_222705.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753453764916-e0b4a318-14c5-4752-b9f2-fc9ad6d5b7a1.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_13%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

大多数情况下，越往东和南，土会越粉，越白，更加沙质

![2.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/53025226/1753456729933-fbbb8914-712b-4ee9-8e5e-05d5df8d1889.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_32%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![局部截取_20250725_223449.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753454505678-17c59918-95a9-4225-ac95-07f319741f60.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_13%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

其房顶多为铁皮，以白色居多，会有反光，靠近郊区也会有黑顶和生锈了的铁皮顶

![局部截取_20250725_222855.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753453785635-bd569807-fbb8-48d8-9326-df8eab391a7a.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_25%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

#### 阿布贾市区

为尼日利亚首都，很繁荣，车水马龙，能见到许多高层公寓楼和豪华别墅，道路平整，其街道相较其他城市更为干净，绿化(行道树）为全尼日利亚最好，建筑的墙体通常以黄色调居多，棕榈树等热带植被鲜见（正常情况下根本看不到）

![局部截取_20250725_220652.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753452480371-71187fac-c0a7-4d22-bdfd-b93bf02320ce.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_30%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

通常情况下，别墅旁会有较高的围墙，围墙上有铁丝网                                                                                  长叶单籽暗罗(Monoon longifolium), 又称假阿育王树，树皮有丰富纤维，纵向剥落。侧枝纤细下垂，枝叶浓密。叶长披针形，边缘波浪状，叶面油亮，四季青翠。在阿布贾及周边的别墅区/富人区非常常见(为下图中高大细长的树）

注：该植被尼日利亚全境可见，但搭配上整洁干净的街道环境仅阿布贾最常见，且阿布贾较常将其作为行道树及道路分隔区绿化使用，其他地方可见但较少

![局部截取_20250725_222312.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753454702178-433d1557-1f3a-4fdf-b81e-68cea7845807.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_22%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

在阿布贾，它会被政府机关用作行道树使用，这在全尼日利亚基本上就阿布贾会比较常见一点(如下图)

![屏幕截图 2025-08-22 161916.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1755850891210-e43dab10-45ed-4de6-85ba-7f8e6d7baaee.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_40%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

#### 阿布贾城郊

在阿布贾城区的周边，通常可以见到装修较好的房屋和少量的农业用地

![局部截取_20250725_221824.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753453147331-0bbe1525-9ef2-4a0e-8a11-cc1dc7dae404.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_29%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

有时，也可以见到一些比较大的施工用地

![局部截取_20250725_221807.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753453467588-9761046b-71fb-4fec-b0f9-50491e83142c.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_28%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

#### 伊杜(Idu)工业区

为联邦首都区最大的工业区，在阿布贾大都会的东边，大致范围如下图

![微信图片_2025-08-17_123254_641.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/53025226/1755405191580-341540e9-92b5-4d23-bdd3-ecc68fa94564.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_38%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

能在周边看到数量，大小可观的工厂(有许多中国公司，你甚至可以见到一些中文标语，如下图第一张)，它们的类型十分多样

![屏幕截图 2025-08-17 123416.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1755405328640-3bf2c226-b583-4e80-b978-9fad2621160d.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_32%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![屏幕截图 2025-08-17 123603.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1755405611632-be6e1c87-b5d0-48c7-8843-0551a28b565c.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_45%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![屏幕截图 2025-08-17 123853.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1755405672227-2bf3034a-1546-4af8-93b5-6de7329baf78.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_45%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![屏幕截图 2025-08-17 123630.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1755405655653-b0bd4788-07b9-4408-ae08-fb6c09378030.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_39%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

在有些路段还可以看到大量的货车

![屏幕截图 2025-08-17 123906.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1755405743214-8808eb83-0a66-453b-a9da-d9a3e4e299e2.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_43%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

值得一提的是，在伊杜工业区的周围能看到大规模的形态相似，排布整齐的毛坯烂尾别墅(通常会有2~4层)

![屏幕截图 2025-08-19 153220.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1755588842126-69466f71-cac7-4e90-889d-95918ea6e7f0.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_43%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

#### 鲁古贝(Lugbe)旁: 一个环岛的世界

下图为Lugbe的所在方位，街景覆盖范围和周边大致地形；图中圈画出的为该Meta所涉及区域

![LLL.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/53025226/1755500389134-c26497a1-e8c3-426b-ae5a-f521189a9a3c.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_53%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

放大后的该区域

![屏幕截图 2025-08-18 150030.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1755500448556-9712b39d-6226-43d2-8db3-e50387dcf2b3.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_42%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

路均为沥青路，周边全是荒地(没有任何人造建筑物在路旁)，可以在西北看到连绵的小山

![屏幕截图 2025-08-18 150143.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1755500566528-b11350e7-988f-4e66-9131-ebf654d09df0.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_49%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

在大多数地方可以在道路尽头看到环岛

![屏幕截图 2025-08-18 150411.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1755500666927-1b3720ac-e315-4170-80aa-3fd91dcfc985.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_29%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

路旁长有大片碧绿的蒯草

![屏幕截图 2025-08-18 150221.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1755500579145-2fc03bc8-6d6a-4cf6-87df-3b160239a283.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_45%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

#### 库布瓦(Kubwa)

下图为Kubwa的所在方位，街景覆盖范围和周边大致地形

![kubwa.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/53025226/1753521863738-f100babb-c630-4c80-a8cb-e6fd31d6ed51.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_17%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

相比较首都，有一种杂乱无章的感觉，景观绿化也很混乱

![局部截取_20250726_171805.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753522073864-9e591a90-1a1c-4c9d-9b93-10316903816f.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_20%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

道路会更加地狭窄和脏乱，房屋不像首都那般豪华，类似于乡村别墅的感觉

![局部截取_20250726_171859.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753522133759-bc426baf-4fa4-4716-8bb2-593e21feef68.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_19%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

通常可以在西边和北边看到较高的山体(连绵成片)，那座山很有标志性，如下图所示

![局部截取_20250726_171953.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753522392955-52b72011-7c4e-4ddb-9f4e-07f00963b5f3.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_19%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

#### 萨博吉比(Sabojibi)

下图为Sabojibi的所在方位，街景覆盖范围和周边大致地形

![kkk.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/53025226/1755500404601-8939322b-ffb5-461e-addb-773d099ce618.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_44%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

太阳有一点点红红的并带给我们雾蒙蒙的氛围感

![屏幕截图 2025-08-18 151123.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1755501098721-77b265d0-d377-42c7-8b67-2590c510f974.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_32%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

周边群山环绕，西南边的山很有标志性

![屏幕截图 2025-08-18 151250.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1755501187649-5eae8d4c-98e6-4572-ae59-d0699a5dc412.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_65%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

#### 库杰(Kuje)

下图为Kuje的所在方位，街景覆盖范围和周边大致地形

![kuje.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/53025226/1753521884064-a26f591a-d463-4d7b-ba77-3ef5ed54b361.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_17%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

比起Kubwa会更加乡下化，杂草丛生，路面基本无铺装

![局部截取_20250726_174022.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753523575841-5977bba5-9e33-480a-a928-0324818313cb.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_17%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

在其南边通常可以看到绵延的高山(这是辨别Kubwa最有效，最直接的办法)

![局部截取_20250726_173833.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753523365335-f13812a9-eb89-4ec2-8b66-52a1713fd578.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_17%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

#### “奶牛”警车跟车

皮卡车，其主体为黑色车身，但因为掉漆(可能是)的缘故，呈现出许多白色的斑点，尤其是车头，在其位于街景车后方时会感到明显的车顶白白的(配色像一只奶牛)；车前的防护栏摇摇欲坠，左低右高；警车顶部的警车车灯的红色部分的最右端有被挤压的痕迹，变得扁扁的。以至于总体看来有点破破烂烂的感觉

![屏幕截图 2025-08-16 225515.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1755356573593-393a7f15-f584-4457-a68a-7664f85a3deb.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_33%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

头顶白白的

![屏幕截图 2025-08-17 105403.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1755399257329-d3365f85-b398-434a-ab12-307de9109ef6.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_13%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

对比，正常的黑皮卡警车

（来源：阿布贾市区的 102 Chinyeaka Ohaa Cres)

![屏幕截图 2025-08-17 105927.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1755399631583-23d32d52-e670-4f39-a3e6-ec42d2897676.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_34%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

它的分布如下图所示，主要是Kuje的东南方,Gwagwalada罕见(基本上仅于其A2公路以东的部分可见)

注：这里只展示其最常见的两个部分，随着谷歌街景的补发，其他地方也有可能见到，但概率较小(几条路的覆盖)，加之景观的介绍，即使不在这两个区块，也可以进行大致区猜

![k.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/53025226/1755496531190-3acf377c-4bbc-49ad-bd27-4c77e091b3b4.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_50%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![微信图片_2025-08-17_125046_194.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/53025226/1755406275877-fd624c14-f132-4a8d-99da-90869f66c615.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_56%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

在该城镇也有少量覆盖

![屏幕截图 2025-08-18 150939.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1755501042222-ca83f89a-eb46-4684-b4a8-1b43deb3bb27.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_26%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

所以，当你认为你在Kuje且看到了该跟车，请点击其东南方向

关于Kalu与Kurudu的辨别，通常来说Kalu作为阿布贾大都会的一个郊区，会更加城市化一点，而Kurudu仅作为阿布贾的一个卫星城市，会更加乡村化一点

#### 赞戈(Zango)及周边

下图为Zango的所在方位，街景覆盖范围和周边大致地形

#### 格瓦瓦拉达-拉皮亚路(Gwagwalada-Lapai Rd)

范围如下图所示

![1.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/53025226/1755604989949-1221dbfa-b437-41e0-8d74-669dbc679d81.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_23%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

它的北段是最好辨识的，可以通过南边高高的山丘，沥青铺路，警车的后视镜缺失和一派绿油油的景象快速辨识出来

![屏幕截图 2025-08-19 200704.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1755605243854-19332524-146a-4ea0-b1c9-475925ed6ced.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_34%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

在沥青路的两旁有平整的黄橙色颗粒状砂土

![屏幕截图 2025-08-19 201100.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1755605497484-b43e57a9-f789-447a-9b81-ad4097896e24.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_59%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

在道路的两旁种有规整的蒯草，蒯草之后则是一片片的嫩绿色的玉米田

![屏幕截图 2025-08-19 201238.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1755605578403-9a1f752c-4f26-45ce-82b0-e6601dec2e1a.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_41%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

#### 机场快速路(Airport Road)

范围如图所示

![lll.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/53025226/1753616546752-286b3faa-651b-47d2-98de-2388fc4ea664.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_30%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

全线都蛮绿的，郁郁葱葱，蓝天白云，天气良好，为分隔式道路且在过机场高架前左右两旁还有辅路

全线基本上是荒郊野岭，周边城镇少(城市化的感觉不及下面要讲的高)

![局部截取_20250727_194459.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753616836145-f6d10701-4cf7-4b9a-a023-29330f26abb0.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_22%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

过机场高架后的路段

![局部截取_20250727_194608.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753617040223-363059c5-1f1a-4958-9cd4-68b5dfa49b35.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

#### 穆尔塔拉·穆罕默德高速公路(Murtala Mohammed Expressway)

范围大体如下，均有分隔护栏加辅路

![ttt.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/53025226/1753618739877-81df3426-3ee8-4daf-9a6f-077eb3e9c1a6.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_30%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

它周边的地形与街景覆盖如下图，在谷歌地图中这条路被标注为A234

![局部截取_20250727_202923.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753619407194-a4319ff4-f7b6-4d28-8737-27365bfd1eed.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_30%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

路上通常会比较繁忙，车水马龙

![局部截取_20250727_202803.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753619453262-fd56a6db-2246-48f6-8b8c-e48d978c9260.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

周围能看到许多大型的城镇聚落​

![局部截取_20250727_202840.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753619510278-1d545945-dc7d-4e51-a32b-6dabde99444f.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

注：上述的两条高速路也可以通过观察周边地形和核对道路走向来辨识

#### A2(联邦首都区段)

比较好找，不展示其范围

为分隔式高速，周边比较干、比较黄

![屏幕截图 2025-08-24 105102.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1756003891815-11251d8b-3faa-478d-9f1d-93b8b0f05ed0.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_44%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

橙红色的太阳并给人一种雾蒙蒙的氛围感

![屏幕截图 2025-08-24 105111.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1756003941955-26f346da-8ec9-4275-a845-1a5be5c64b2c.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_34%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

### 联邦首都区北部

联邦首都区北部(范围小,不是很重要,但依旧建议看看,至少混个眼熟)

![kkk.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/53025226/1753535765075-1dcf6108-e60f-49b1-9eeb-06025c8cd7cb.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_14%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

#### 总体环境

周边有许多小黄花(可能是矢车菊)

![局部截取_20250726_182202.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753546617449-ec0ab855-94c3-41b9-8c98-50214402c187.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_16%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

也有许多类似蒲草/芦苇荡的植被

![局部截取_20250726_182114.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753546690223-11245f68-512b-406c-a3ec-7141fda27099.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_15%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

它们通常会交错生长在一起

![局部截取_20250727_001201.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753546769875-e212c0ea-542a-483d-9d49-7536bd0e77ec.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

周边的山会比较多，山上有成片的草(黄绿色或枯黄色)，有稀疏的树木伴生

![局部截取_20250727_001424.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753546837674-79a820dd-b119-4ec2-a31d-86db1a29774e.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_23%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

山上常见裸露在外的岩石，外表较为光滑，有轻微的层裂现象

![局部截取_20250727_001615.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753546862563-38cb78eb-8566-4939-9dd7-310c2f7771a1.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_23%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

#### 塔莎-布瓦里快速路(Tasha-Bwari Express Rd)

周围地形与范围大致如下图所示

注:该快速路在华为地图上并没有全线标为分隔式道路，请不要相信它(华为地图)

它在环岛后，取消分隔式护栏

![aaa.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/53025226/1753534420122-c5f9d2fb-94e7-40f0-94d4-0d59a9a7d3ca.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_13%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

为该区域内唯一的分隔式道路，周边多山

![局部截取_20250727_001251.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753547898860-2dcc5a62-a78b-4557-91db-8b118368bf89.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

北段的分隔护栏如下图，它会比南段更橙些，中间通常是一些土壤的填充

![局部截取_20250727_003413.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753617691481-da46ba08-a734-47ad-89fc-1fa2d262eb7e.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_20%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

#### 乌沙帕(Ushapa)

周围地形与范围大致如下图所示

![局部截取_20250727_005020.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753548651698-33b63c30-bf06-42ac-aac1-e434b5fa4d02.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_20%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

在城镇的房屋周围总有一块一块的荒草杂乱地生长，虽道路狭窄，房屋间距小，但却给人一种空旷的感觉

![局部截取_20250727_004916.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753548575154-6437f472-d483-4881-b2e3-42fb67a762fc.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_22%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

这里的太阳似乎有一圈红边，给人带来一种雾蒙蒙的感觉

![局部截取_20250727_013739.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753551482538-4db9421e-0eea-4841-bb74-4a106bfff5f1.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_11%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

### 卡杜纳州

邀请你来图寻做「卡杜纳州G4」题库 [https://tuxun.fun/map/40313](https://tuxun.fun/map/40313)

卡杜纳州的大致位置与街景覆盖情况，如下图

![局部截取_20250731_131721.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753939149843-ce71d6d3-3aaf-493c-8aa6-3c4a72c6e876.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_13%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![Kaduna_State_Nigeria.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1756013375046-ae572f35-f753-4ae1-8575-fbb816571cdc.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_12%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

由于卡杜纳州的四代覆盖多为城市乡村间的道路，景观差异较小且多为全码车覆盖，总体难度较大，故本章将会介绍较多跟车的Meta

注：在该州99.99%+的题目中，你只能见到以辆全码车(卡车)(如下图)

![屏幕截图 2025-08-27 125402.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1756270459225-8f06f3d6-037c-41d1-9aff-55b5cc399d2f.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_48%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

#### 总体环境

在卡杜纳州，80%以上的野外题都可以见到一堆一堆的干草垛，这是辨认该州最直接，最简单的办法，因为在尼日利亚，这种干草垛几乎仅该州可见

![局部截取_20250730_145820.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753859019969-8e028d65-6ea4-47ca-8cb0-44e35cdb34d4.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_16%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

相较于同纬度东部的各州，它的植被覆盖率很高；相较于联邦首都区，地形更加平坦，远离道路两旁的草会更高(非农业区)；在该州也可以见到蒯草，但较少见，通常不会大片分布

![局部截取_20250731_132100.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753939292821-48c77e55-e3a5-4313-bbaa-31ab36a56d40.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_23%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

也会有许多玉米种植

![局部截取_20250731_133057.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753939903831-bce1e038-9463-4445-bb04-8d9283bbda6d.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_24%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

蒯草比起联邦首都区可能会更绿?

![屏幕截图 2025-08-21 145400.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1755763106650-76d0df9b-008f-48d0-9f68-ae50c3c4e06b.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_35%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

开阔的景观，树木在数量比联邦首都区多很多

![屏幕截图 2025-08-21 145432.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1755763171700-6a6fdbc2-4f51-403b-bf4e-6148ed56487f.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_38%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

#### 卡杜纳(Kaduna)

​

#### 卡杜纳州主路四代覆盖跟车总览

见下图

由于卡杜纳州的景观总体差异较小，学习其主要道路的跟车以更好地区猜该州还是十分必要的

![屏幕截图 2025-08-27 123535.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1756269377463-b293e605-c762-4fdc-a007-1eb1463ded64.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_30%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

红色：黑色警车

湖水蓝/青绿：普通白车有护栏

浅蓝色：普通白车无护栏

绿色：白缺有护栏

黄色：白缺无护栏

蓝色：多街景车同时存在(因一些重复项，无法在此图完全展示)

备注：在该州的许多地方存在多辆车同时拍摄的情况

注意：仅讲解主要道路，一小段一小段的小土路由于出现频次少、记忆麻烦，故在这里不作讲解，感兴趣的可自行研究

接下来会详细展示

##### 黑色警车

如下图，主要分布在南方和北部的一小块部分，A235靠近卡杜纳(Kaduna)的一小块覆盖可忽略不计

![屏幕截图 2025-08-27 124529.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1756269943803-5d373f26-db2d-46bb-9c6f-da555c8178de.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_28%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

其样式见下图

![屏幕截图 2025-08-27 125731.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1756270695391-c7fb2db7-acf9-4801-841c-9bdebdafb2f8.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_14%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

黑车覆盖详解部分

A11(华为地图标注为A236)一直到塔玛B(Tama B)，及向北两条铺装较好的道路

![屏幕截图 2025-08-27 130251.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1756271005603-3454b509-6130-4b8d-8a5a-1b7333051d55.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_29%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

分布在卡恰A235以东、卡恰-宗夸路、卡凡钱A235南部、卡戈罗和考拉东南、考拉和曼乔克北部

##### 多街景车同时存在

如下图，主要在A2、A236部分可见，其他地方也有少量分布

![屏幕截图 2025-08-27 134535.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1756273622957-262855ce-dfa1-45e3-87a9-7ab66bf56093.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_27%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

详解部分​

先解释一下概念，顾名思义，就是该路段由多辆街景车拍摄，分两种情况

1.其他街景车或其跟车在你可视范围内同时你能看见你所处这辆街景车的跟车，如下图

![屏幕截图 2025-08-27 135453.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1756274269193-303ac463-0e03-468e-915e-9cba3890a7d5.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_13%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

2.其他街景车或其跟车在你可视范围内但你似乎看不见你自己的跟车，如下图

该情况仅出现在前文所提及未被重复覆盖的蓝色部分

![屏幕截图 2025-08-27 135105.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1756274334604-39362ebd-e775-4790-b780-2009102ab4cd.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_12%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

注：在南部，黑车跟车也有这种情况，但因为它开得太快了，仅能从其他街景车上看到它的黑色跟车，从它那看不到/看不清(无法辨识)其他街景车，故不属于此类情况

之后的部分将以此为基础详细讲解道路、城市的辨识

#### 南部区域总体辨识

大致范围见下图

![屏幕截图 2025-08-27 141135.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1756275867825-c8fdb85d-5cbf-40db-9ef0-50f63f692db9.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_37%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

总的来讲就是很南边的氛围、环境，你能看见一些让人感觉比较热带的植被，生锈发红的铁皮顶也更为常见。同时，卡杜纳州那经典的干草垛在这里将更为少见甚至于基本看不到

![屏幕截图 2025-08-27 141722.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1756275486480-421c4e99-65ad-412d-b4cf-1889e072258c.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_50%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![屏幕截图 2025-08-27 141732.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1756275833185-075c7347-0708-4d01-9853-7000afd08f38.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_33%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

有时可以在周围看到大片的树林，整体会比较绿

![屏幕截图 2025-08-27 203122.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1756298001774-3e832286-dfed-443a-a0df-6827fb961572.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_51%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

#### 卡戈罗(Kagoro)及考拉(Kaura)的总体辨识

大致区域见下图

![屏幕截图 2025-08-27 202925.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1756297788795-8c35cfbc-23ad-4905-8670-c63f204b5ea2.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_38%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

刷新在乡间小路，周边偶尔有些高大的玉米田

![屏幕截图 2025-08-27 195908.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1756296007299-8d2ce3eb-9901-4d9c-8aeb-e106264c5274.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_46%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

最重要的是，你可以在你的南边看到连绵的高大山脉，通过这点可以帮您快速地判断出该区域

![屏幕截图 2025-08-27 195857.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1756296124682-69d70952-10c1-48d3-ac13-5f833555efea.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_68%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

#### (待完成)卡恰(Kachia)

#### (待完成)卡恰周边的小路

#### A125(Kaduna-Buruku)

如下图所示

![屏幕截图 2025-09-07 114917.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1757216974139-47b2dd3b-517b-45c6-8dc6-940802229402.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_49%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

白色普通警车跟车，很阴沉的天气，周边的树木成排排列，并且让人感到有一种不像正常卡杜纳州的氛围

沥青路面，但有时会有许多泛白的条纹，常常可以看见裂纹

![屏幕截图 2025-09-07 115023.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1757217049852-aebede99-0271-41b5-a225-8a780166e66b.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_46%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

越往东走，前面所述的那种氛围感就会更强，下图就是一个很好、很典型的例子

![屏幕截图 2025-09-07 115555.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1757217376478-36dfe6b7-3a0d-4e2b-9fe3-57de05c6aea0.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_53%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

#### A235中段(Kurmi-kachia)

跟车参照上文

范围如图所示

![1.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1757218962264-35e7cd1c-2e88-48d8-90bd-f82ed6881ff5.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_35%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

该段中间

### 关于土壤盐碱化，(不用知道也行)阅读下方须知

#### 涉及地区

北部主要为以下六州

#### 成因

以下六州都主要位于尼日利亚干旱的苏丹草原带(Sudan Savanna)，年降水量普遍低于800mm，旱季漫长，使土壤存在钠盐累计的现象

#### 表现特征(重要)

不同地区所呈现的特征略有差异，但大体都有以下特征

1.会有些许颗粒状的砂石和轻微的浅层坑洞

2.有明显的颗粒分散，结构松散的感觉

3.通常情况下，盐碱化越严重的土壤表面的植被(大多是细如头发丝的青绿色矮草)覆盖越稀疏

### 高原州(PTA)

邀请你来图寻做「高原州」题库 [https://tuxun.fun/map/40314](https://tuxun.fun/map/40314)

高原州四代街景的大致覆盖范围如下

![屏幕截图 2025-08-24 103413.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1756002925974-e41dcd66-9895-4ec1-b762-6f97133fbaa1.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_23%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![Plateau_State_Nigeria.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1756003444162-bec5c54c-ae03-4f82-bbdd-73e1a2c2bc84.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_12%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

#### 总体环境

高原州的山上基本上都能看到许多裸石，而且不论是从近处看还是从远处看，这些裸石都会给人一种非常稀碎零散的感觉；山上的植被覆盖基本上也只有一些稀疏的小草，偶尔会夹杂着一些小型灌木，很难在山上看到中大型树木

![局部截取_20250731_140941.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753942217516-b4739b91-5b7d-46a8-b75b-f7285cd0be86.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_26%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![局部截取_20250731_140953.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753942236841-f5af1a24-71b1-4ee7-9803-9354d45d5aae.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_29%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

郊区/市区农田，比较干旱，有极其轻微的盐碱化

即田地旁甚至田地中会有青绿色的小草(真的非常小)

![局部截取_20250731_142320.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1753943029335-c2a0be81-ac98-479d-b33c-9068032d79c3.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_20%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

有时，在郊区的地里会有零散的大块岩石裸露

![屏幕截图 2025-08-15 142036.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1755238946458-3c1dc51c-0018-4a7c-84c8-40086db4aeb6.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_43%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

郊区屋顶以白色银色为主，鲜见黑色，深绿色

装修较好的别墅会附有土墙

![屏幕截图 2025-08-15 142859.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1755239358468-d444d10e-300b-4854-b212-cf947ac02e2a.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_59%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

在市区也可以见到数量可观的生锈了的铁皮顶

![屏幕截图 2025-08-15 143552.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1755239768417-a1d58d26-996d-476c-b577-fd56a1f404a6.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_54%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

#### 嘟嘟车和出租车

嘟嘟车在高原州非常常见，因大致细节在上章联邦首都区已介绍，就不多概述

如下图，它会在它的前轮全涂绿，其他特征细节请自行观看

通常来讲它会在车身上写有高原州(Plateau State)的英文简写PTA

位置通常在下图所示的两个位置

![屏幕截图 2025-08-15 143959.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1755240078432-382b3e66-eb17-4842-bc68-caa7fbdd78ce.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_20%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![屏幕截图 2025-08-15 144024.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1755240086932-036e2593-debd-404a-a39f-5719b520c55c.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_13%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

出租车在高原州非常少见，几乎只在Jos的市中心附近可以看到，涂装如下

（可能有其他的变体)

![屏幕截图 2025-08-15 143908.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1755240276952-73731008-1f3f-4aac-8032-db247e62ab2e.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_37%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

#### 西南湖区总体景观辨识

范围大体如下(水库or湖,我也不知道,就且当它是湖吧)

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1756191339583-f8374b09-6397-4344-916d-0c523abf5ce5.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_29%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

异常地空旷，村庄、房屋较少，多为开阔的田地和稀疏的树木

![屏幕截图 2025-08-26 145726.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1756191494411-e14c0eb6-c998-4d7c-a6ba-52cc1ad790c9.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_55%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

有略微的起伏，土壤颜色多为红褐色，可以见到许多嫩绿色的小草

![屏幕截图 2025-08-26 145739.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1756191598056-578fad78-571a-4fab-916f-c684607b1de0.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_54%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

关于该区域的道路辨别，将会在本章末尾谈及

#### 红车覆盖

红皮卡覆盖如下

分别是在Jos的西北角

![1.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1769525156390-a0cf5de6-dafc-447f-9291-368c02330129.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_46%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

和Jos的东南角

![33.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/53025226/1756022673673-319a5a01-83ec-40a8-8bd0-4413a3cc363a.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_43%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

其中红车80%以上的覆盖都是阴天拍摄的，大致氛围如下图

![屏幕截图 2025-08-24 160834.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1756022962880-5fba9ad0-11ff-4e4c-85aa-f10bddbaca1b.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_46%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

而晴天覆盖非常少，仅主要集中在覆盖的最东南角的地方(Turu和K Vom附近)，覆盖范围如下图，大致在绿色框内

![55.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/53025226/1756046037214-ce2b4b5c-80a3-4075-949a-3b63a715a7ba.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_43%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

晴天覆盖的大致氛围见下图

![屏幕截图 2025-08-24 160852.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1756023117828-b9eb3aee-18bf-4154-9925-633640536f26.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_45%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

这将帮助我们精准定位

晴天覆盖地区没有阴天覆盖，阴天覆盖地区没有晴天覆盖

道路识别将会在后续内容中提及

#### 乔斯(Jos)市区

其市区核心区范围大体如下，主要是由A236(橙色)、A3(黄色)和Ring Rd(最北的深灰色)构成的三角地带，越往南越繁荣

![屏幕截图 2025-08-24 223511.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1756046185613-07da0be1-7bff-4421-ad77-f18f0e6e5def.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_16%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

可以通过车水马龙的街道，较矮的小公寓楼以及装修较为精致、外表干净的别墅辨识

![屏幕截图 2025-08-24 161951.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1756023651209-bb29078c-80c0-4344-a89f-80f9c09b741e.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_53%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

整个Jos及Jos以北的区域都给人以一种泛黄的感觉

![屏幕截图 2025-08-24 162003.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1756023833694-a5d3f54d-d8bd-498d-99b7-742f3fdfdd51.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_51%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

#### 库鲁(Kuru)

范围大体如下

![2.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1769525485936-bdb12315-1c1c-4e59-8c20-53292603dacd.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_40%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

喀麦隆大戟（Euphorbia kamerunica）是大戟科的一种开花植物。它分布于非洲萨赫勒地区，包括尼日利亚、喀麦隆、乍得和埃塞俄比亚。在尼日利亚中部，大戟属植物（Euphorbia kamerunica）被用作围栏。它的刺对动物来说很危险，其有毒的乳状汁液也能阻止大型动物进出。该植物在Jos郊区非常常见

![屏幕截图 2026-02-01 113136.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1769917476279-b1764039-fbc1-45f8-b638-13c310dfd5c0.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_26%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![屏幕截图 2026-02-01 113445.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1769917488890-0b4fc8c6-92a6-48c2-85b9-290591a36cd3.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_41%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

当地人使用其作为围栏/篱笆

![屏幕截图 2026-02-01 125449.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1769921705859-284391e5-b6f7-4a4d-99cb-ad3a6d1976f9.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_48%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

扇叶棕/糖棕(Borassus flabellifer) 是一种健壮的乔木，可高达30米（98英尺）。树干呈灰色，粗壮，布满叶痕

在Jos郊区也很常见

![屏幕截图 2026-02-01 114950.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1769937003683-aff184ba-5488-4d53-b221-3c8d3a1bb08f.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_22%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

有一种雾蒙蒙、橙橙的调调

![屏幕截图 2026-02-01 125906.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1769921982844-bbe7dcd3-3e43-4b27-bbf7-c3e5e56b51d7.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_47%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

周围有一些小山丘，土壤为橙色、橙黄色

范围如图所示

这种小路(狭窄的微橙的沙质道路加上道路两旁紧凑的大戟围栏)，通常在Turu西边靠山的一带比较常见

#### 巴希特(Bahit)

范围如图所示

![1.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1770806429601-fc267c49-f495-44d4-800b-11583d7a2d56.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_60%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

可见到红车，全码车两种类型的街景车

全码车给人的调调类似于前文述及的土路，有村庄的感觉

![屏幕截图 2026-02-11 190714.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1770808097733-25000b0e-207f-4912-9487-a73804355c8c.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_54%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

红车见下，可以通过土壤(橙红色)大致分辨

![屏幕截图 2026-02-11 190859.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1770808185212-699ec4e0-da90-4fed-b97e-30b143b36399.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_55%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

最主要的辨别方式还是通过北边的山

![屏幕截图 2026-02-11 191209.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1770808355494-adeb185b-4b42-416b-849d-25b1e3fa9437.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_51%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

它与南边的红车分布区的小区别：大戟围栏很少见，即便有也通常给人一种瘦小的样子

![屏幕截图 2026-02-11 191153.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1770808597385-b9dcfccd-4931-4f9d-9a3d-f05dcc9e62b5.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_51%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

#### 嘟嘟车(和出租车?)

此类型的标准嘟嘟车(位于包奇)在这三州/四州均可见且最为常见，出租车几乎见不到

特点就是全车均为黄色涂装

关于这些标准嘟嘟车的辨别,主要通过缩写的不同，缩写、编号颜色的差异，一些细节差异来区分

![屏幕截图 2026-02-12 172631.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1770888410348-8a05b822-a37f-4358-96d5-8121605dc02b.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_30%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![屏幕截图 2026-02-12 172357.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1770888298041-e3c5d6c3-5111-45dd-a6c5-002774e68944.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_44%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

其中，不同州的嘟嘟车各自在车身会标有该州的缩写

包奇州(BAU)缩写多用黑漆，编号多用红漆

![屏幕截图 2026-02-12 172440.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1770888967266-550d2876-01eb-4936-aead-924975c65e97.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_40%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

贡贝州(GMT)缩写和编号都多用黑漆书写

![屏幕截图 2026-02-12 175444.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1770890368711-d10ed4ff-63e4-43d6-91e6-877bc02cbc87.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_33%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

此外，贡贝州还流行一种全绿色的新型(新?)嘟嘟车(不缩小了，给大家大饱眼福)

(不难看出，就是在原嘟嘟车基础上改装而来的  绿色漆掉了里面居然是黄色的)

![屏幕截图 2026-02-12 175235.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1770890525905-7cbad008-8e9d-4f9b-bf10-4cbfce9fe680.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_48%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

绿色嘟嘟车成群结队地驶来

![屏幕截图 2026-02-12 175502.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1770890816722-714c2e52-e3a8-40ef-9fd3-aa51c452f685.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_50%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

阿扎雷(KBY)，缩写和编号多用绿色漆书写​

![屏幕截图 2026-02-12 181106.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1770891475729-14b57ead-0e04-4b56-8b3a-f35644dda636.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_41%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

约贝州(有点特殊)

以下分别为波蒂斯库姆(Potiskum)(上图)和达马图鲁(Damaturu)(下图)的嘟嘟车

Potiskum：编号和缩写均多用蓝漆书写，缩写似乎并非约贝州缩写，而为该城市的缩写(PKM)

Damaturu：编号多用绿漆，缩写非常小(尽管Potiskum的PKM已经够小了)

![屏幕截图 2026-02-12 173005.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1770892445159-7c42ffe1-250c-4aaf-9eaa-253e95897b28.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_38%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![屏幕截图 2026-02-12 173244.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1770892426952-5ef6403e-e5d1-49d7-9249-af976dbdbb72.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_32%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

（当然，编号和缩写也有被码到看不清的时候,故这里再介绍一个区分出约贝州的方法)

在约贝州，嘟嘟车的两个车灯下基本上都有个白色的矩形，矩形内填充有该车辆的缩写和编号信息

正如前面所述的那样，左图为Potiskum，右图为Damaturu.

![屏幕截图 2026-02-12 232713.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1770910150292-e120e5ed-e3de-4a9e-b57d-afea2d666dbb.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_25%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![屏幕截图 2026-02-12 232512.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1770910249026-b42254bb-4526-4756-9338-60dd4595e264.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

一辆出租车?来自Damaturu.

#### 包奇(Bauchi)郊区

能够看到许多椰枣（Phoenix dactylifera）

![屏幕截图 2025-08-14 142108.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1755154686792-a9d310f6-0de2-4a30-bffb-cd3fac67faa2.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_37%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

能看到大量的有大面积的岩石裸露的山丘，山上的植被相较高原州更加稀少，并且给人一种干干的、灰灰的氛围感

![屏幕截图 2025-08-14 142132.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1755154706347-d2d26aec-4e2c-4c9b-942e-8073a5050a8a.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_51%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

环境十分干旱，土壤有轻度的盐碱化​

![屏幕截图 2025-08-14 142144.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/53025226/1755154716288-0d0e73cb-a36a-48ee-883c-1c0f597c0f5b.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_39%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

#### 贡贝-波蒂斯库姆路(Combe-Potiskum Rd)

范围如下，向北行驶

![1.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1771165219899-139a76a8-04ea-4fe3-b232-78d0efa6c266.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_36%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

它在拍摄时似乎经历了天气的变化，由阴转晴

故分为两段，其中绿色段大致为阴天，黄色段大致为晴天

![屏幕截图 2026-02-15 222550.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1771165598582-3a42af43-b94e-4a7a-a3be-6133c1752dc6.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_37%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

快到Potiskum时

如上三图所示，从Gombe到Potiskum，周围的景观也急剧变化

大致变化可参照上三图，都非常典型

下面介绍一种特殊的电线杆(整个北部散见，下面的范围仅对于这条路来说)，深褐色金属的柱子和倒三角形的杆顶支撑结构(绝缘体类型不必在意)

右图为普通的混凝土电线杆

![屏幕截图 2026-02-15 223914.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1771166837152-b7ac4c8c-1fad-4a30-b31e-e704b638dd40.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_14%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![屏幕截图 2026-02-15 224947.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1771167009555-a44a295d-fffd-4040-ba46-3f62be497c92.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_14%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

它主要分布在如下区域

#### 总体环境

极易识别的独特的环境

植被分布稀疏且不连续，以低矮的灌木丛、草丛为主，夹杂着零散的高大树木。以广阔的平原和缓坡地形为主，土地多为红褐色或浅棕色，地表裸露程度较高，部分区域可见明显的土坡或平坦荒地，呈现典型的稀树草原（萨凡纳）地貌

环境总体给人一种广袤、自然、略带荒凉的感觉

![屏幕截图 2026-02-16 125610.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1771217818257-9f6e7614-b5d2-4ded-ac6d-e8ba3b4ce5f9.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_50%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![屏幕截图 2026-02-16 125544.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1771217812729-959d0717-6e85-4e01-9319-329fc497714c.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_48%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

#### 嘟嘟车

普通的黄色嘟嘟车

![屏幕截图 2026-02-16 162144.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1771230121579-dfeb31ab-609c-4903-ba26-41f9d4fb6438.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_20%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

于Jimeta

Jalingo的嘟嘟车侧边写有PT-000X(三个数字加一个字母)，用黑漆写成

且车窗的右上方(对于司机)，通常有黑色的文字

范围如下

## Part3 东部

### 克罗斯/十字河流州和阿夸伊博姆州

范围如下

![屏幕截图 2026-02-20 124507.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1771562735059-b1ac2d07-558e-4dc6-8868-4b1ee9e0e122.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_59%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![屏幕截图 2026-02-20 124608.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1771562789254-a2e6d62d-cfe3-4da0-9eb4-8f690c4cf6d5.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_53%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

#### 总体环境

在尼日利亚的东南部分布着尼日利亚最广阔、最大的油棕森林，成片的油棕在这里随处可见，西南相较这里，油棕会少见非常多

![屏幕截图 2026-02-18 203226.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1771418092132-300cdfd8-10a8-4532-a97a-698321709fae.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_52%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

这种略微泛白的沙质土壤也非常具有标志性

![屏幕截图 2026-02-18 203240.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1771418113979-574a3355-05e7-4f41-a7a4-8d5de3b2832a.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_42%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

#### 嘟嘟车和出租车

克罗斯河州(Cross River)的嘟嘟车为深蓝色/墨蓝色，编号多为五位数字，用白漆涂写

![屏幕截图 2026-02-18 205102.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1771419141107-0f6ecd9c-7cdc-4632-9293-ad40c78f674b.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_40%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

阿夸伊博姆州的嘟嘟车为大红色

![屏幕截图 2026-02-19 113228.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1771471961764-f2e0cb6b-6925-4438-8f4c-ff4b595d53f6.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_20%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

阿夸伊博姆州的出租车的车身配色也以红色为主，且车型多为面包车

![屏幕截图 2026-02-19 191540.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1771499900970-24c215a8-f30e-4d28-b1a4-9abadb182462.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_34%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

其他地方的造型可能略有差异，不变的是那令人醒目的红色

![屏幕截图 2026-02-19 191701.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1771499914233-e2f3681a-fbc7-4625-8aca-e2d9edf70011.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_44%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

#### 卡拉巴尔(Calabar)

卡拉巴尔的地形和街景覆盖见下

![屏幕截图 2026-02-19 114113.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1771499352656-1a1c4502-7df8-41ef-a36e-724ecfcb956f.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_15%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

路面会有一点泛白

![屏幕截图 2026-02-19 113737.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1771474323734-7a2a81e1-25ff-4776-960b-e7517c323263.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_47%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

这种房屋在Calabar非常常见，五颜六色的铁皮顶和房屋外墙，以及极具辨识度的带有青苔的石头外墙

![屏幕截图 2026-02-19 113750.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1771474346864-dd931bd0-f93c-4069-81c5-8f974d62c14b.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_33%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

这种石头外墙配上干净的街道在Calabar很常见

![屏幕截图 2026-02-19 121628.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1771474645550-02293582-b084-4042-b2ff-bb7bee098446.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_48%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

典型的Calabar街头

![屏幕截图 2026-02-19 113827.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1771475209605-f9d7e495-fc59-47f6-b6c2-17f757da03b2.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_45%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

凤凰木（[学名](https://zh.wikipedia.org/wiki/%E5%AD%A6%E5%90%8D)：Delonix regia，英语：Poinciana）因鲜红或橙色的花朵配合鲜绿色的羽状复叶，被誉为世上最色彩鲜艳的树木之一，叶片是二回羽状[复叶](https://zh.wikipedia.org/wiki/%E8%A4%87%E8%91%89)，呈羽片[对生](https://zh.wikipedia.org/wiki/%E5%B0%8D%E7%94%9F)，15-30对，每羽片有小叶20-40对。小叶为长椭圆形，基部歪斜，[叶缘](https://zh.wikipedia.org/wiki/%E8%91%89%E7%B7%A3)是全缘，叶端圆钝。[叶片](https://zh.wikipedia.org/wiki/%E8%91%89%E7%89%87)是薄纸质，叶面平滑且薄，为青绿色，[叶脉](https://zh.wikipedia.org/wiki/%E5%8F%B6%E8%84%89)则仅中肋明显。树形为广阔伞形

它们在Calabar极其常见，在四代拍摄时，凤凰木未到开花的时节

![屏幕截图 2026-02-19 121738.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1771497748011-de3ce084-d831-4509-9e90-6b0a2cb4ff30.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_34%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

典型的Calabar的主路，绿意盎然

![屏幕截图 2026-02-19 114230.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1771497945996-6b4d9b8c-e778-4168-8630-21c024a12722.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_44%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

### 埃努古州、贝努埃州、埃邦伊州

范围如下

#### 总体环境

可以参考Plonk It教程中有关贝努埃州的部分，而这样的环境在埃努古州和埃邦伊州也很常见

这种翠绿青葱的草(下图道路两旁)是辨别出该地区的最有效、最直接的方法

![屏幕截图 2026-02-19 215510.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1771509336923-11983319-5f65-4e93-acf6-11a2ae113e12.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_48%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

在比较南或比较北的地区，它们可能会比较矮一些，但这并不妨碍我们认出它们来

![屏幕截图 2026-02-19 220008.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1771509696839-e22d6079-b1ce-49db-ad45-f86b2d8f9505.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_36%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

当然，仅凭这些仍无法准确辨识Okposi，所以笔者仍建议遇到类似环境直接点居中的Abakaliki

#### 关于水泥路

这种类似于菲律宾、泰国的水泥路面在埃邦伊州最为常见(95%)

大多数水泥路是可识别的，但笔者仍在研究

![屏幕截图 2026-02-20 134507.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1771566424905-edc779fd-ac68-48e9-93c8-bd7581fef7d0.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_48%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

## 区猜部分

### 东南乌约(Uyo)周边(适用于整个阿夸伊博姆州)

### 乌穆阿希亚(Umuahia)周边

![屏幕截图 2026-02-21 205651.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1771678999658-4172dc2f-e1ad-4f08-89ec-b8ae83c5528e.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_16%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

土壤泛红且较为沙质

![屏幕截图 2026-02-21 205515.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1771678684668-091ce574-dc7e-4007-8c4a-4150eed74d7f.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_50%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

通常油棕遍布，在居住区中，给人感觉较为开阔，多为白色警车跟车

### (待完成)奥维里(Owerri)周边

### 内维(Nnewi)周边

![屏幕截图 2026-02-21 210359.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1771679353952-f1d27b2f-6d2b-4aad-8533-072a58992364.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_23%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

道路两旁的排水沟在这周边很常见，多为黑色警车跟车

![屏幕截图 2026-02-21 210428.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1771679119689-234cc753-9d4b-4bae-8025-8a83c9b7d87d.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_51%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

道路周边与Umuahia不同，建筑物、植被啥的比较紧凑

![屏幕截图 2026-02-21 210557.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1771679252494-a0a1c5f6-8563-438d-b396-284f9060cf91.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_42%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

这种紧凑的氛围加上路两旁微微泛红的沙质路面能让你快速锁定这里

# 第五章   老Shitcam

## 绪论

它的分布如下图所示，除了几条路补了一下覆盖，其他的大差不差

![](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2024/png/35193536/1712942274027-67dcb283-ad27-497d-98bd-944d37370046.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_68%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_68%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

Vibe见下

![屏幕截图 2026-02-23 160046.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1771833667440-226aa1e9-c132-4250-9137-7bec9dfa96a9.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_43%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

## 区猜部分

### 玉米地

这种很绿很绿的成片的玉米地通常可以在卡诺州和卡杜纳州附近见到

一定要注意，很多人常常会因此而误点南方

![屏幕截图 2026-02-23 224910.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1771858501776-37c9df63-3cd3-406d-9f0f-58d9fc6944e8.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_52%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![屏幕截图 2026-02-23 225022.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1771858749095-3e664e06-52ca-4e16-aeae-386334bdf316.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_54%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

如果你还看到了卡杜纳州标志性的干草垛，你大概率在扎里亚(Zaria)的附近，且Zaria的西边sc覆盖更多

![屏幕截图 2026-02-23 225210.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1771858746918-b8de721e-640b-4216-adaf-b564337abc54.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_49%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

### 杜切(Dutse)的沙漠小路

![屏幕截图 2026-02-23 230124.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1771859307451-8c651f87-35f9-4c32-a3c5-9f89e8854710.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_28%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

行驶在干旱沙漠中的小土路在Dutse的南边最常见，土壤偏黄色

![屏幕截图 2026-02-23 230054.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1771858967084-e5948f57-39ab-4670-ae7a-8f8f3921f816.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_55%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![屏幕截图 2026-02-23 230101.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1771859107219-0dd9b775-a2db-489b-9c42-c326e74259fb.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_53%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

### 卡诺(Kano)

![屏幕截图 2026-02-23 230712.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1771859256284-2d0ec72c-4817-4162-9a91-ed37632ab65c.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_15%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

### 索科托(Sokoto)

![屏幕截图 2026-02-23 231245.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1771859583337-12da8403-4c20-4091-a5f4-adf4ccdc65de.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_31%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

SC中最好识别的城市

土壤相较同纬度的其他城市红非常多，这种红壤放眼整个尼日利亚都是独一无二的存在

![屏幕截图 2026-02-23 231124.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1771859562268-cb86fdc7-8ada-48b6-86f5-781e47400ab8.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_50%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

## 区猜部分

### 卡诺州(Kano)

沙漠景观

![屏幕截图 2026-02-24 101438.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1771899307714-97ad46d8-062c-4d22-8add-c115bcd2cf70.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_51%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

### 三角洲州(Delta)

![屏幕截图 2026-02-24 101629.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1771900176025-add268d9-2065-4303-8b9e-3ea73ea9edc6.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_38%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

通常来说是一辆黑色街景车或一辆银车(银车通常有天线)

路两旁有白白的沙土，绿意盎然，有很多南方的植被(通常会比较密集)

如果你出现在一条又隔离带的修缮完好的分隔式道路上时，你大概率在河流州(哈科特港周边)和阿夸伊博姆州的南边

![屏幕截图 2026-02-24 101551.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1771899523644-5e408729-c73d-4c77-a81e-e53718d12e90.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_46%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![屏幕截图 2026-02-24 101857.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1771899661526-896bab7d-a6af-43a9-9e24-92f29d413370.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_47%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

### 河流州(River)的灰色调

![屏幕截图 2026-02-24 104009.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1771900984007-59699faf-e54a-4b71-9437-bf754481b50f.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_17%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

集中于河流州北部，很明显的氛围

![屏幕截图 2026-02-24 104226.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1771901058971-1455ceb7-5272-4751-845e-475d5ab944b9.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_46%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![屏幕截图 2026-02-24 104213.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1771901042618-941673c7-66b5-42da-abec-4e2ebe168506.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_61%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

### 纳萨拉瓦州(Nasarawa)的灰色调

![1.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1771901353726-95778e4c-432a-4e5e-9e84-f735f6413c02.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_41%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

### 凯恩吉湖国家公园(Kainji Lake National Park)附近

![屏幕截图 2026-02-24 102329.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/png/53025226/1771899829515-8c24b6c2-c38f-4b2b-b808-983b9724e4ce.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_42%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

# 附录

## 一、相关网站

1.首先是一些尼日利亚官方的部分网站，虽然他们对于区猜研究并没有什么帮助

[https://agriculture.gov.ng](https://agriculture.gov.ng/)  尼日利亚联邦农业和粮食安全部官网

[https://environment.gov.ng](https://environment.gov.ng/) 尼日利亚联邦环境部官网

[https://frin.gov.ng](https://frin.gov.ng/) 尼日利亚林业研究所(FRIN)官网

（其他的就不一一列举了）

2.论文查找

[https://www.ajol.info/index.php/ajol](https://www.ajol.info/index.php/ajol) 非洲在线期刊(AJOL)

## 二、相关文章,书籍和图

[https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/16iweF1-vourV5yWrbKltsKjcNDv_I3GwOBVusHCTdtU/htmlview](https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/16iweF1-vourV5yWrbKltsKjcNDv_I3GwOBVusHCTdtU/htmlview)  一篇国外的尼日利亚相关文档，但个人认为没什么用

[https://www.fao.org/soils-portal/data-hub/soil-maps-and-databases/global-map-of-salt-affected-soils/en](https://www.fao.org/soils-portal/data-hub/soil-maps-and-databases/global-map-of-salt-affected-soils/en/) 联合国粮食及农业组织(FAO)的盐渍土地图

托因 法洛拉《尼日利亚史》(The History of Nigeria),沐涛,译,上海：东方出版中心,2015  给了我诸多启发

关于植被，跳转

[https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scirpus_cyperinus](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scirpus_cyperinus) 香附子/蒯草（Scirpus cyperinus）

[https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Monoon_longifolium](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Monoon_longifolium) 长叶暗罗（Monoon longifolium）

[https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Euphorbia_kamerunica](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Euphorbia_kamerunica)  喀麦隆大戟（Euphorbia kamerunica）

[https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Borassus_flabellifer](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Borassus_flabellifer) 扇叶棕/糖棕（Borassus flabellifer）

[https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Date_palm](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Date_palm) 椰枣树（Phoenix dactylifera）

[https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Delonix_regia](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Delonix_regia) 凤凰木（Delonix regia）
